</tr>
<tr style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border-color: rgb(204, 204, 204) currentcolor currentcolor; border-style: solid none none; border-width: 1px 0px 0px; border-image: none 100% / 1 / 0 stretch; background-color: white;">

</tr>
<tr style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border-color: rgb(204, 204, 204) currentcolor currentcolor; border-style: solid none none; border-width: 1px 0px 0px; border-image: none 100% / 1 / 0 stretch; background-color: white;">
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">bzip2</td>
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">org.apache.hadoop.io.compress.BZip2Codec</td>
</tr>
<tr style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border-color: rgb(204, 204, 204) currentcolor currentcolor; border-style: solid none none; border-width: 1px 0px 0px; border-image: none 100% / 1 / 0 stretch; background-color: white;">
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">LZO</td>
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">com.hadoop.compression.lzo.LzopCodec</td>
</tr>
<tr style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border-color: rgb(204, 204, 204) currentcolor currentcolor; border-style: solid none none; border-width: 1px 0px 0px; border-image: none 100% / 1 / 0 stretch; background-color: white;">
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">Snappy</td>
<td style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; font-size: 1em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204); padding: 0.5em 1em; text-align: left;">org.apache.hadoop.io.compress.SnappyCodec</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">压缩性能的比较</p>

<h3 id="h113" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(0, 116, 217); margin-bottom: 50px; font-size: 1em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; display: inline-block; background: rgb(0, 116, 217) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); padding: 10px 16px; border-radius: 5px; box-shadow: rgb(0, 116, 217) 5px 5px 10px;">11.3 压缩方式选择</span></h3>
<pre style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><code class="properties language-properties" style="overflow-wrap: break-word; padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0px 2px; color: rgb(233, 105, 0); background: rgb(248, 248, 248) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; line-height: 18px; font-size: 14px; font-weight: normal; word-spacing: 0px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-family: Consolas, Inconsolata, Courier, monospace; border-radius: 0px; white-space: pre !important; word-wrap: normal !important; word-break: normal !important; overflow: auto !important; display: -webkit-box !important;">【压缩】<br>优点：压缩率比较高，而且压缩/解压速度也比较快；hadoop&nbsp;本身支持，在应用中处理gzip&nbsp;格式的文件就和直接处理文本一样；大部分&nbsp;linux&nbsp;系统都自带&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;命令，使用方便。<br>缺点：不支持&nbsp;split。<br>应用场景：当每个文件压缩之后在&nbsp;130M&nbsp;以内的（1&nbsp;个块大小内），都可以考虑用&nbsp;gzip压缩格式。例如说一天或者一个小时的日志压缩成一个&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;文件，运行&nbsp;mapreduce&nbsp;程序的时候通过多个&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;文件达到并发。hive&nbsp;程序，streaming&nbsp;程序，和&nbsp;java&nbsp;写的&nbsp;mapreduce&nbsp;程序完全和文本处理一样，压缩之后原来的程序不需要做任何修改。<br><br>【Bzip2&nbsp;压缩】<br>优点：支持&nbsp;split；具有很高的压缩率，比&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;压缩率都高；hadoop&nbsp;本身支持，但不支持native；在&nbsp;linux&nbsp;系统下自带&nbsp;bzip2&nbsp;命令，使用方便。<br>缺点：压缩/解压速度慢；不支持&nbsp;native。<br>应用场景：适合对速度要求不高，但需要较高的压缩率的时候，可以作为&nbsp;mapreduce&nbsp;作业的输出格式；或者输出之后的数据比较大，处理之后的数据需要压缩存档减少磁盘空间并且以后数据用得比较少的情况；或者对单个很大的文本文件想压缩减少存储空间，同时又需要支持&nbsp;split，而且兼容之前的应用程序（即应用程序不需要修改）的情况。<br><br>【Lzo&nbsp;压缩】<br>优点：压缩/解压速度也比较快，合理的压缩率；支持&nbsp;split，是&nbsp;hadoop&nbsp;中最流行的压缩格式；可以在&nbsp;linux&nbsp;系统下安装&nbsp;lzop&nbsp;命令，使用方便。<br>缺点：压缩率比&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;要低一些；hadoop&nbsp;本身不支持，需要安装；在应用中对&nbsp;lzo&nbsp;格式的文件需要做一些特殊处理（为了支持&nbsp;split&nbsp;需要建索引，还需要指定&nbsp;inputformat&nbsp;为&nbsp;lzo&nbsp;格式）。<br>应用场景：一个很大的文本文件，压缩之后还大于&nbsp;200M&nbsp;以上的可以考虑，而且单个文件越大，lzo&nbsp;优点越越明显。<br><br>【Snappy&nbsp;压缩】<br>优点：高速压缩速度和合理的压缩率。<br>缺点：不支持&nbsp;split；压缩率比&nbsp;gzip&nbsp;要低；hadoop&nbsp;本身不支持，需要安装；<br>应用场景：当&nbsp;Mapreduce&nbsp;作业的&nbsp;Map&nbsp;输出的数据比较大的时候，作为&nbsp;Map&nbsp;到&nbsp;Reduce&nbsp;的中间数据的压缩格式；或者作为一个&nbsp;Mapreduce&nbsp;作业的输出和另外一个&nbsp;Mapreduce&nbsp;作业的输入。<br></code></pre>
<h3 id="h114" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(0, 116, 217); margin-bottom: 50px; font-size: 1em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; display: inline-block; background: rgb(0, 116, 217) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); padding: 10px 16px; border-radius: 5px; box-shadow: rgb(0, 116, 217) 5px 5px 10px;">11.4 压缩位置选择</span></h3>
<ol style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: decimal;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em; color: rgb(233, 105, 0);"><p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">在有大量数据并计划重复处理的情况下，应考虑对输入进行压缩，map的输入一般采用bzip2，支持切片。</p></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em; color: rgb(233, 105, 0);"><p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">当map输出的中间数据量很大时，可以选择LZO或者Snappy进行压缩。</p></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em; color: rgb(233, 105, 0);"><p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">减少存储的数据量，降低所需的磁盘空间，reduce输出使用gzip压缩，不支持切片</p></li>
</ol>
<h3 id="h115" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(0, 116, 217); margin-bottom: 50px; font-size: 1em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; display: inline-block; background: rgb(0, 116, 217) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); padding: 10px 16px; border-radius: 5px; box-shadow: rgb(0, 116, 217) 5px 5px 10px;">11.5 压缩案例实操</span></h3>
<h4 id="h1" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">1. 数据流的压缩和解压缩</span></h4>
<pre style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><code class="java language-java hljs" style="overflow-wrap: break-word; margin: 0px 2px; line-height: 18px; font-size: 14px; font-weight: normal; word-spacing: 0px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-family: Consolas, Inconsolata, Courier, monospace; border-radius: 0px; overflow-x: auto; padding: 0.5em; background: rgb(40, 42, 54) none repeat scroll 0% 0%; color: rgb(248, 248, 242); white-space: pre !important; word-wrap: normal !important; word-break: normal !important; overflow: auto !important; display: -webkit-box !important;"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">package</span>&nbsp;cool.xiaokang.compress;<br><br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;org.apache.hadoop.conf.Configuration;<br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;org.apache.hadoop.fs.Path;<br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;org.apache.hadoop.io.compress.CompressionCodec;<br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;org.apache.hadoop.io.compress.CompressionCodecFactory;<br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;org.apache.hadoop.util.ReflectionUtils;<br><br><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">import</span>&nbsp;java.io.*;<br><br><span class="hljs-comment" style="font-size: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(139, 233, 253); font-weight: bold; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">class</span>&nbsp;<span class="hljs-title" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; <h4 id="h3reduce" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">3. Reduce输出端采用压缩</span></h4>
